Here goes:\n\n```cpp\n#include <bits/stdc++.h>\nusing namespace std;\nusing namespace chrono;\n\nstatic int J, M, nOps;\nstatic vector<vector<int>> jM, jD; // machine, duration for each job/op\nstatic vector<int> jW; // total work per job\nstatic vector<int> off; // offset[j] = start id for job j ops\nstatic vector<int> oJ, oP; // decode: opId -> (j, p)\nstatic vector<int> jobSuccArr; // jobSuccArr[id] = id of job successor (-1 if none)\nstatic vector<int> baseDeg; // base in-degree from job constraints\n\nvoid init() {\n    off.resize(J+1, 0);\n    for(int j=0;j<J;j++) off[j+1]=off[j]+(int)jM[j].size();\n    nOps=off[J];\n    oJ.resize(nOps); oP.resize(nOps);\n    jobSuccArr.assign(nOps,-1);\n    baseDeg.assign(nOps,0);\n    for(int j=0;j<J;j++) {\n        for(int p=0;p<(int)jM[j].size();p++) {\n            int id=off[j]+p;\n            oJ[id]=j; oP[id]=p;\n            if(p>0) baseDeg[id]=1;\n            if(p+1<(int)jM[j].size()) jobSuccArr[id]=id+1;\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nusing MO=vector<vector<pair<int,int>>>;\n\n// Working arrays (reused across eval calls)\nstatic vector<int> wa_machPred, wa_machSucc, wa_inDeg, wa_est, wa_bfsQ, wa_topo, wa_lft;\nvoid allocW() {\n    wa_machPred.resize(nOps); wa_machSucc.resize(nOps);\n    wa_inDeg.resize(nOps); wa_est.resize(nOps);\n    wa_bfsQ.resize(nOps); wa_topo.resize(nOps); wa_lft.resize(nOps);\n}\n\n// Returns makespan (-1 if cycle)\n// If doLST: fills wa_lft with LST values\nint eval(const MO& mo, bool doLST=false) {\n    fill(wa_machPred.begin(),wa_machPred.end(),-1);\n    fill(wa_machSucc.begin(),wa_machSucc.end(),-1);\n    for(int m=0;m<M;m++) {\n        const auto& v=mo[m];\n        for(int k=1;k<(int)v.size();k++) {\n            auto [j,p]=v[k];\n            auto [pj,pp]=v[k-1];\n            int u=off[j]+p, w=off[pj]+pp;\n            wa_machPred[u]=w;\n            wa_machSucc[w]=u;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    // Compute inDeg\n    copy(baseDeg.begin(),baseDeg.end(),wa_inDeg.begin());\n    for(int i=0;i<nOps;i++) {\n        int mp=wa_machPred[i];\n        if(mp>=0) {\n            int j=oJ[i],p=oP[i];\n            if(!(p>0 && mp==off[j]+p-1)) // not same as job pred\n                wa_inDeg[i]++;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    fill(wa_est.begin(),wa_est.end(),0);\n    int head=0,tail=0;\n    for(int i=0;i<nOps;i++) if(!wa_inDeg[i]) wa_bfsQ[tail++]=i;\n    int topoSz=0;\n    \n    while(head<tail) {\n        int u=wa_bfsQ[head++];\n        if(doLST) wa_topo[topoSz]=u;\n        topoSz++;\n        int j=oJ[u],p=oP[u];\n        int et=wa_est[u]+jD[j][p];\n        int v=jobSuccArr[u];\n        if(v>=0) {\n            if(et>wa_est[v]) wa_est[v]=et;\n            if(!--wa_inDeg[v]) wa_bfsQ[tail++]=v;\n        }\n        int w=wa_machSucc[u];\n        if(w>=0 && w!=v) {\n            if(et>wa_est[w]) wa_est[w]=et;\n            if(!--wa_inDeg[w]) wa_bfsQ[tail++]=w;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    if(topoSz<nOps) return -1; // cycle\n    \n    int ms=0;\n    for(int i=0;i<nOps;i++) {\n        int e=wa_est[i]+jD[oJ[i]][oP[i]];\n        if(e>ms) ms=e;\n    }\n    \n    if(doLST) {\n        fill(wa_lft.begin(),wa_lft.end(),ms);\n        for(int i=topoSz-1;i>=0;i--) {\n            int u=wa_topo[i];\n            int j=oJ[u],p=oP[u];\n            int lstU=wa_lft[u]-jD[j][p];\n            if(p>0) { int v=off[j]+p-1; if(lstU<wa_lft[v]) wa_lft[v]=lstU; }\n            int w=wa_machPred[u];\n            if(w>=0) { if(lstU<wa_lft[w]) wa_lft[w]=lstU; }\n        }\n        for(int i=0;i<nOps;i++) wa_lft[i]-=jD[oJ[i]][oP[i]];\n    }\n    return ms;\n}\n\nMO extractMO(const vector<vector<int>>& s) {\n    MO mo(M);\n    vector<vector<pair<int,pair<int,int>>>> tmp(M);\n    for(int j=0;j<J;j++)\n        for(int p=0;p<(int)jM[j].size();p++)\n            tmp[jM[j][p]].push_back({s[j][p],{j,p}});\n    for(int m=0;m<M;m++) {\n        sort(tmp[m].begin(),tmp[m].end());\n        for(auto& [t,jp]:tmp[m]) mo[m].push_back(jp);\n    }\n    return mo;\n}\n\nvector<vector<int>> getStart(const MO& mo) {\n    eval(mo);\n    vector<vector<int>> s(J);\n    for(int j=0;j<J;j++) {\n        s[j].resize(jM[j].size());\n        for(int p=0;p<(int)jM[j].size();p++) s[j][p]=wa_est[off[j]+p];\n    }\n    return s;\n}\n\n// Greedy: priority 0=MWKR, 1=SPT, 2=LPT\nvector<vector<int>> greedy(int pri) {\n    vector<int> remWork=jW;\n    vector<vector<int>> s(J);\n    for(int j=0;j<J;j++) s[j].resize(jM[j].size());\n    vector<int> nxt(J,0), rdy(J,0), mf(M,0);\n    vector<bool> um(M);\n    \n    for(int sch=0; sch<nOps; ) {\n        int t=INT_MAX;\n        for(int j=0;j<J;j++) {\n            if(nxt[j]>=(int)jM[j].size()) continue;\n            int st=max(mf[jM[j][nxt[j]]],rdy[j]);\n            if(st<t) t=st;\n        }\n        \n        vector<pair<int,int>> cands;\n        for(int j=0;j<J;j++) {\n            if(nxt[j]>=(int)jM[j].size()) continue;\n            int m=jM[j][nxt[j]];\n            if(max(mf[m],rdy[j])!=t) continue;\n            int key;\n            if(pri==0) key=-remWork[j];\n            else if(pri==1) key=jD[j][nxt[j]];\n            else key=-jD[j][nxt[j]]; // LPT\n            cands.push_back({key,j});\n        }\n        sort(cands.begin(),cands.end());\n        \n        fill(um.begin(),um.end(),false);\n        for(auto [key,j]:cands) {\n            int p=nxt[j];\n            int m=jM[j][p];\n            if(um[m]) continue;\n            um[m]=true;\n            int d=jD[j][p];\n            s[j][p]=t;\n            mf[m]=t+d;\n            rdy[j]=t+d;\n            remWork[j]-=d;\n            nxt[j]++;\n            sch++;\n        }\n    }\n    return s;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    ios::sync_with_stdio(false);\n    cin.tie(nullptr);\n    \n    cin>>J>>M;\n    jM.resize(J); jD.resize(J); jW.resize(J,0);\n    for(int j=0;j<J;j++) {\n        int T; cin>>T;\n        jM[j].resize(T); jD[j].resize(T);\n        for(int p=0;p<T;p++) {\n            cin>>jM[j][p]>>jD[j][p];\n            jW[j]+=jD[j][p];\n        }\n    }\n    \n    init(); allocW();\n    \n    // Run multiple greedy heuristics\n    auto s0=greedy(0); // MWKR\n    auto mo0=extractMO(s0);\n    int ms0=eval(mo0);\n    \n    auto s1=greedy(1); // SPT\n    auto mo1=extractMO(s1);\n    int ms1=eval(mo1);\n    \n    auto s2=greedy(2); // LPT  \n    auto mo2=extractMO(s2);\n    int ms2=eval(mo2);\n    \n    MO bestMO; int bestMs=INT_MAX;\n    for(auto& [mo,ms]: vector<pair<MO,int>>{{mo0,ms0},{mo1,ms1},{mo2,ms2}}) {\n        if(ms<bestMs) { bestMs=ms; bestMO=mo; }\n    }\n    \n    // Time-limited local search\n    auto tStart=steady_clock::now();\n    auto elapsed=[&](){ return duration_cast<duration<double>>(steady_clock::now()-tStart).count(); };\n    \n    // Decide time limit based on size\n    double tl;\n    if(nOps<=300) tl=8.0;\n    else if(nOps<=3000) tl=5.0;\n    else if(nOps<=15000) tl=2.0;\n    else tl=0.5;\n    \n    // Tabu search\n    if(tl>0.1) {\n        int tenure=max(5, min(20, J/2));\n        vector<vector<int>> tabu(M);\n        for(int m=0;m<M;m++) tabu[m].assign(max(1,(int)bestMO[m].size()),0);\n        \n        MO curMO=bestMO;\n        int curMs=bestMs;\n        int iter=0;\n        \n        while(elapsed()<tl) {\n            // Get current solution\'s EST and LST\n            int ms=eval(curMO, true);\n            if(ms<0) break;\n            \n            vector<int> cEst=wa_est, cLst=wa_lft; // save copies\n            \n            bool found=false;\n            int bGain=INT_MIN;\n            int bM=-1, bK=-1;\n            bool bIsTabu=false;\n            \n            for(int m=0;m<M && elapsed()<tl;m++) {\n                auto& v=curMO[m];\n                for(int k=0;k+1<(int)v.size() && elapsed()<tl;k++) {\n                    auto [j1,p1]=v[k];\n                    auto [j2,p2]=v[k+1];\n                    int u=off[j1]+p1, w=off[j2]+p2;\n                    \n                    // CP filter (for large instances)\n                    if(nOps>200) {\n                        bool uCP=(cEst[u]==cLst[u]);\n                        bool wCP=(cEst[w]==cLst[w]);\n                        if(!uCP && !wCP) continue;\n                    }\n                    \n                    // Try swap\n                    swap(v[k],v[k+1]);\n                    int newMs=eval(curMO);\n                    swap(v[k],v[k+1]);\n                    \n                    if(newMs<0) continue;\n                    \n                    bool isTabu=(k<(int)tabu[m].size() && tabu[m][k]>iter);\n                    int gain=ms-newMs;\n                    \n                    if(!isTabu) {\n                        if(!found || gain>bGain) {\n                            found=true; bGain=gain; bM=m; bK=k; bIsTabu=false;\n                        }\n                    } else if(newMs<bestMs) { // aspiration\n                        if(!found || !bIsTabu || gain>bGain) {\n                            found=true; bGain=gain; bM=m; bK=k; bIsTabu=true;\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n            \n            if(!found) break;\n            \n            auto& v=curMO[bM];\n            swap(v[bK],v[bK+1]);\n            curMs=eval(curMO);\n            if(bK<(int)tabu[bM].size()) tabu[bM][bK]=iter+tenure;\n            iter++;\n            \n            if(curMs>0 && curMs<bestMs) {\n                bestMs=curMs;\n                bestMO=curMO;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    // Get start times from bestMO\n    auto bestStart=getStart(bestMO);\n    \n    // Output\n    for(int j=0;j<J;j++) {\n        for(int p=0;p<(int)jM[j].size();p++) {\n            if(p>0) cout<<\' \';\n            cout<<bestStart[j][p]<<\' \'<<jM[j][p];\n        }\n        cout<<\'\\n\';\n    }\n    \n    return 0;\n}\n```\n\nWait, there are some issues:\n1. `for(auto& [mo,ms]: vector<pair<MO,int>>{{mo0,ms0},{mo1,ms1},{mo2,ms2}})` - this copies MO objects, which is expensive. Let me just use if-else.\n\n2. The tabu list size `tabu[m].assign(max(1,(int)bestMO[m].size()),0)` might not cover all positions if bestMO changes. Better to size it by max machine queue length or just by nOps.\n\n3. The copy `vector<int> cEst=wa_est, cLst=wa_lft` allocates new vectors each iteration. For performance, preallocate these.\n\n4. The `elapsed()<tl` check inside the nested loop might cause timing issues (the check itself takes time). For performance, check only every N iterations.\n\nLet me also reconsider the CP filter. For the backward pass, `wa_lft` stores LST (latest start time). A node u is on the critical path if `wa_est[u] == wa_lft[u]`.\n\nWait, I need to double check. After the backward pass:\n- `wa_lft[i]` starts as `ms` (makespan)\n- We compute: for each node u in reverse topo order, `lstU = wa_lft[u] - jD[j][p]`, then update predecessors: `wa_lft[pred] = min(wa_lft[pred], lstU)`\n- Finally: `wa_lft[i] -= jD[oJ[i]][oP[i]]`\n\nSo after the backward pass conversion, `wa_lft[i]` = latest start time of op i.\n\nAnd `wa_est[i]` = earliest start time of op i.\n\nCritical path: ops where `wa_est[i] == wa_lft[i]`.\n\nThis should be correct.\n\nLet me trace through the example again:\nJob 0: (M0, d=3), (M1, d=2)\nJob 1: (M1, d=2), (M0, d=4)\n\nOpIds: op0=(0,0)=0, op1=(0,1)=1, op2=(1,0)=2, op3=(1,1)=3\n\nMO (from greedy): M0: [(0,0),(1,1)], M1: [(1,0),(0,1)]\n\nmachPred: mp[0]=-1, mp[1]=2, mp[2]=-1, mp[3]=0\nmachSucc: ms[0]=3, ms[1]=-1, ms[2]=1, ms[3]=-1\njobSuccArr: js[0]=1, js[1]=-1, js[2]=3, js[3]=-1\nbaseDeg: [0,1,0,1]\ninDeg: [0, 1+1(mach pred 2, not dup since p=1 but mp=2≠off[0]+0=0... wait let me recalculate]\n\nop0=(j=0,p=0): baseDeg=0, machPred=-1, inDeg=0\nop1=(j=0,p=1): baseDeg=1, machPred=2(≠off[0]+0=0 so not dup), inDeg=1+1=2\nop2=(j=1,p=0): baseDeg=0, machPred=-1, inDeg=0\nop3=(j=1,p=1): baseDeg=1, machPred=0(≠off[1]+0=2-1=... wait off[1]=2, so off[1]+p-1=off[1]+0=2, but p=1 means p-1=0, off[j]+p-1=2+0=2 ≠ 0). So not dup. inDeg=1+1=2\n\nForward pass:\n- Init: bfsQ=[0,2] (inDeg=0)\n- Process 0: j=0,p=0,dur=3,et=3. jobSucc=1: est[1]=max(0,3)=3, inDeg[1]=2-1=1. machSucc=3: est[3]=max(0,3)=3, inDeg[3]=2-1=1.\n- Process 2: j=1,p=0,dur=2,et=2. jobSucc=3: est[3]=max(3,2)=3, inDeg[3]=1-1=0→push. machSucc=1: est[1]=max(3,2)=3, inDeg[1]=1-1=0→push.\n- Process 3 (inDeg=0): j=1,p=1,dur=4,et=7. jobSucc=-1. machSucc=-1. \n- Process 1 (inDeg=0): j=0,p=1,dur=2,et=5. jobSucc=-1. machSucc=-1.\n\nEST: [0,3,0,3]\nMakespan = max(3,5,2,7) = 7 ✓\n\nBackward pass:\n- lft = [7,7,7,7]\n- Process in reverse topo order: [1, 3, 2, 0]\n  - Process 1 (j=0,p=1): lstU=7-2=5. p>0: lft[off[0]+0=0]=min(7,5)=5. machPred=2: lft[2]=min(7,5)=5.\n  - Process 3 (j=1,p=1): lstU=7-4=3. p>0: lft[off[1]+0=2]=min(5,3)=3. machPred=0: lft[0]=min(5,3)=3.\n  - Process 2 (j=1,p=0): lstU=(after converting) wait, we haven\'t converted yet. At this point, lft[2]=3 (LFT). lstU=3-2=1. p=0: no job pred. machPred=-1: nothing.\n  - Process 0 (j=0,p=0): lft[0]=3 (LFT). lstU=3-3=0. p=0: nothing. machPred=-1: nothing.\n- Convert LFT to LST: lft[i] -= jD[oJ[i]][oP[i]]\n  - lft[0]=3-3=0, lft[1]=7-2=5, lft[2]=3-2=1, lft[3]=7-4=3\n\nLST: [0, 5, 1, 3]\nEST: [0, 3, 0, 3]\n\nCritical path: EST[i]==LST[i]:\n- op0: 0==0 ✓ on CP\n- op1: 3==5? No. Not on CP.\n- op2: 0==1? No. Not on CP.\n- op3: 3==3 ✓ on CP\n\nCritical machine arcs:\n- M0: [(0,0),(1,1)] → (op0,op3). op0 on CP, op3 on CP → critical arc! ✓\n- M1: [(1,0),(0,1)] → (op2,op1). op2 not on CP, op1 not on CP → not critical.\n\nThis matches my earlier analysis. The swap (op0,op3) on M0 was tried and found to be worse (makespan 11 > 7). So we keep the current solution.\n\nThe code logic looks correct.\n\nNow let me also think about the validity of the output. The schedule must be valid (no overlaps, precedence respected). My greedy scheduler produces a valid schedule. The local search uses `eval` which correctly computes EST given machine orders, and the resulting schedule should be valid.\n\nBut let me verify: the EST computed by `eval` for a given machine order - is it guaranteed to be a valid schedule?\n\nEST[u] is the maximum of:\n- Job predecessor\'s finish time\n- Machine predecessor\'s finish time (via machine order)\n\nSo:\n- EST[u] ≥ finish time of job pred (j,p-1): ✓ job order respected\n- EST[u] ≥ finish time of machine pred: ✓ machine order respected, no overlap on machine\n\nBut is the machine order non-overlapping? If ops are in the order given by the machine list, and each starts after the previous finishes, then yes.\n\nSo the `eval` function gives a valid schedule for any valid machine ordering (acyclic). ✓\n\nAlright, I think the code is logically correct. Let me now finalize and clean it up.\n\nOne issue I notice: the tabu list might not be correctly sized. Initially, I size it to `bestMO[m].size()`, but as the search progresses and curMO changes, some indices might be out of bounds.\n\nFix: size the tabu list to `max possible operations per machine`. The maximum is nOps (if all ops are on the same machine), but typically nOps/M. Let me just use nOps as the size:\n\n```cpp\nvector<vector<int>> tabu(M, vector<int>(nOps, 0));\n```\n\nThis is safe but wastes memory for large M. For M=50 and nOps=50k, that\'s 50*50k = 2.5M integers = 10MB. Acceptable.\n\nActually, each machine has at most J ops (one per job), so the machine order size is at most J. For J=1000 and M=50, that\'s 50*1000 = 50k integers = 200KB. Much more reasonable.\n\n```cpp\nvector<vector<int>> tabu(M, vector<int>(J+1, 0));\n```\n\nThis is safe because each machine has at most J ops, so indices are in [0, J-1].\n\nOK, let me now write the final clean version. I\'ll include one more thing: a perturbation mechanism to escape local optima. When the tabu search finds no improving move for many iterations, I\'ll perturb the current solution.\n\nPerturbation: randomly swap some consecutive pairs on randomly chosen machines.\n\nBut this might not be necessary for the problem. I\'ll make it clean and compile-ready:\n\nActually, I want to reconsider one thing about the critical path filter in the tabu search. My filter is:\n```cpp\nbool uCP=(cEst[u]==cLst[u]);\nbool wCP=(cEst[w]==cLst[w]);\nif(!uCP && !wCP) continue;\n```\n\nThis means: include the swap if at least one of the two ops is on the CP. This is more inclusive than the strict "both on CP" filter.\n\nThe strict filter (both on CP) corresponds to the N1/N7 neighborhood of Nowicki & Smutnicki and is guaranteed to not create cycles.\n\nThe relaxed filter (at least one on CP) includes more neighbors but might miss some productive swaps.\n\nActually for correctness, let me just try all consecutive pairs (no CP filter) for small instances and CP filter for large:\n\n```cpp\nbool useCP=(nOps>500);\nif(useCP && !uCP && !wCP) continue;\n```\n\nOK one more thing: the tabu tenure. The typical tenure for JSSP is around 5-15. I used `max(5, min(20, J/2))`. For J=2, this gives max(5, 1) = 5. For J=100, this gives max(5, 20) = 20. Seems reasonable.\n\nAlright, let me write the final code now. I\'ll combine everything:\n\nActually, I realize I have a potential performance issue in the greedy: using `vector<pair<int,int>> cands` with dynamic allocation inside the loop. Let me use a static/pre-allocated array.\n\nHere\'s my truly final version of the code. I\'ll write it cleanly:\n\n```cpp\n#include <bits/stdc++.h>\nusing namespace std;\nusing namespace chrono;\nusing namespace std::chrono;\n\nstatic int J, M, nOps;\nstatic vector<vector<int>> jM, jD; // machine[j][p], duration[j][p]\nstatic vector<int> jW; // total work per job\nstatic vector<int> off; // off[j] = start op id for job j\nstatic vector<int> oJ, oP; // oJ[id]=job, oP[id]=pos\nstatic vector<int> jSucc; // jSucc[id] = id of next op in same job (-1 if last)\nstatic vector<int> bDeg; // base in-degree (from job constraints)\n\nvoid init() {\n    off.resize(J+1, 0);\n    for(int j=0;j<J;j++) off[j+1]=off[j]+(int)jM[j].size();\n    nOps=off[J];\n    oJ.resize(nOps); oP.resize(nOps);\n    jSucc.assign(nOps,-1);\n    bDeg.assign(nOps,0);\n    for(int j=0;j<J;j++) {\n        for(int p=0;p<(int)jM[j].size();p++) {\n            int id=off[j]+p;\n            oJ[id]=j; oP[id]=p;\n            if(p>0) bDeg[id]=1;\n            if(p+1<(int)jM[j].size()) jSucc[id]=id+1;\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nusing MO=vector<vector<pair<int,int>>>;\n\nstatic vector<int> wMP,wMS,wID,wE,wQ,wT,wL;\nvoid allocW() { wMP.resize(nOps);wMS.resize(nOps);wID.resize(nOps);wE.resize(nOps);wQ.resize(nOps);wT.resize(nOps);wL.resize(nOps); }\n\nint eval(const MO& mo, bool doL=false) {\n    fill(wMP.begin(),wMP.end(),-1);\n    fill(wMS.begin(),wMS.end(),-1);\n    for(int m=0;m<M;m++) {\n        const auto& v=mo[m];\n        for(int k=1;k<(int)v.size();k++) {\n            int u=off[v[k].first]+v[k].second;\n            int w=off[v[k-1].first]+v[k-1].second;\n            wMP[u]=w; wMS[w]=u;\n        }\n    }\n    copy(bDeg.begin(),bDeg.end(),wID.begin());\n    for(int i=0;i<nOps;i++) {\n        int mp=wMP[i];\n        if(mp>=0) {\n            int j=oJ[i],p=oP[i];\n            if(!(p>0 && mp==off[j]+p-1))\n                wID[i]++;\n        }\n    }\n    fill(wE.begin(),wE.end(),0);\n    int h=0,t=0;\n    for(int i=0;i<nOps;i++) if(!wID[i]) wQ[t++]=i;\n    int sz=0;\n    while(h<t) {\n        int u=wQ[h++];\n        if(doL) wT[sz]=u;\n        sz++;\n        int j=oJ[u],p=oP[u];\n        int et=wE[u]+jD[j][p];\n        int v=jSucc[u];\n        if(v>=0) { if(et>wE[v]) wE[v]=et; if(!--wID[v]) wQ[t++]=v; }\n        int w=wMS[u];\n        if(w>=0&&w!=v) { if(et>wE[w]) wE[w]=et; if(!--wID[w]) wQ[t++]=w; }\n    }\n    if(sz<nOps) return -1;\n    int ms=0;\n    for(int i=0;i<nOps;i++) { int e=wE[i]+jD[oJ[i]][oP[i]]; if(e>ms) ms=e; }\n    if(doL) {\n        fill(wL.begin(),wL.end(),ms);\n        for(int i=sz-1;i>=0;i--) {\n            int u=wT[i]; int j=oJ[u],p=oP[u];\n            int lu=wL[u]-jD[j][p];\n            if(p>0) { int v=off[j]+p-1; if(lu<wL[v]) wL[v]=lu; }\n            int w=wMP[u]; if(w>=0) { if(lu<wL[w]) wL[w]=lu; }\n        }\n        for(int i=0;i<nOps;i++) wL[i]-=jD[oJ[i]][oP[i]];\n    }\n    return ms;\n}\n\nMO toMO(const vector<vector<int>>& s) {\n    MO mo(M);\n    vector<vector<pair<int,pair<int,int>>>> tmp(M);\n    for(int j=0;j<J;j++)\n        for(int p=0;p<(int)jM[j].size();p++)\n            tmp[jM[j][p]].push_back({s[j][p],{j,p}});\n    for(int m=0;m<M;m++) {\n        sort(tmp[m].begin(),tmp[m].end());\n        for(auto& [t,jp]:tmp[m]) mo[m].push_back(jp);\n    }\n    return mo;\n}\n\nvector<vector<int>> toStart(const MO& mo) {\n    eval(mo);\n    vector<vector<int>> s(J);\n    for(int j=0;j<J;j++) { s[j].resize(jM[j].size()); for(int p=0;p<(int)jM[j].size();p++) s[j][p]=wE[off[j]+p]; }\n    return s;\n}\n\nvector<vector<int>> greedy(int pri) {\n    vector<int> rW=jW;\n    vector<vector<int>> s(J); for(int j=0;j<J;j++) s[j].resize(jM[j].size());\n    vector<int> nx(J,0),rd(J,0),mf(M,0);\n    static vector<pair<int,int>> cands;\n    vector<bool> um(M);\n    for(int sc=0;sc<nOps;) {\n        int t=INT_MAX;\n        for(int j=0;j<J;j++) {\n            if(nx[j]>=(int)jM[j].size()) continue;\n            int st=max(mf[jM[j][nx[j]]],rd[j]); if(st<t) t=st;\n        }\n        cands.clear();\n        for(int j=0;j<J;j++) {\n            if(nx[j]>=(int)jM[j].size()) continue;\n            int m=jM[j][nx[j]];\n            if(max(mf[m],rd[j])!=t) continue;\n            int k=(pri==0)?-rW[j]:(pri==1)?jD[j][nx[j]]:-jD[j][nx[j]];\n            cands.push_back({k,j});\n        }\n        sort(cands.begin(),cands.end());\n        fill(um.begin(),um.end(),false);\n        for(auto [k,j]:cands) {\n            int p=nx[j],m=jM[j][p];\n            if(um[m]) continue; um[m]=true;\n            int d=jD[j][p];\n            s[j][p]=t; mf[m]=t+d; rd[j]=t+d; rW[j]-=d; nx[j]++; sc++;\n        }\n    }\n    return s;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    ios::sync_with_stdio(false); cin.tie(nullptr);\n    cin>>J>>M;\n    jM.resize(J); jD.resize(J); jW.resize(J,0);\n    for(int j=0;j<J;j++) {\n        int T; cin>>T; jM[j].resize(T); jD[j].resize(T);\n        for(int p=0;p<T;p++) { cin>>jM[j][p]>>jD[j][p]; jW[j]+=jD[j][p]; }\n    }\n    init(); allocW();\n    \n    // Multiple greedy solutions\n    MO bestMO; int bestMs=INT_MAX;\n    for(int pri:vector<int>{0,1,2}) {\n        auto s=greedy(pri);\n        auto mo=toMO(s);\n        int ms=eval(mo);\n        if(ms<bestMs) { bestMs=ms; bestMO=mo; }\n    }\n    \n    // Time-limited tabu search\n    auto t0=steady_clock::now();\n    auto elapsed=[&](){ return duration_cast<duration<double>>(steady_clock::now()-t0).count(); };\n    \n    double tl=(nOps<=500)?8.0:(nOps<=5000)?5.0:(nOps<=15000)?2.0:0.5;\n    \n    if(tl>0.1 && nOps>0) {\n        int tenure=max(5,min(25,J/3));\n        MO cur=bestMO; cL.resize(nOps);\n        \n        while(elapsed()<tl) {\n            int ms=eval(cur,true);\n            if(ms<0) break;\n            copy(wE.begin(),wE.end(),cE.begin());\n            copy(wL.begin(),wL.end(),cL.begin());\n            \n            bool found=false;\n            int bG=INT_MIN,bM=-1,bK=-1;\n            bool bTab=false;\n            \n            for(int m=0;m<M&&elapsed()<tl;m++) {\n                auto& v=cur[m];\n                int vsz=(int)v.size();\n                for(int k=0;k+1<vsz&&elapsed()<tl;k++) {\n                    int u=off[v[k].first]+v[k].second;\n                    int w=off[v[k+1].first]+v[k+1].second;\n                    // CP filter\n                    if(nOps>300) {\n                        if(cE[u]!=cL[u]&&cE[w]!=cL[w]) continue;\n                    }\n                    // Try swap\n                    swap(v[k],v[k+1]);\n                    int nm=eval(cur);\n                    swap(v[k],v[k+1]);\n                    if(nm<0) continue;\n                    bool iT=(k<(int)tab[m].size()&&tab[m][k]>iter);\n                    int g=ms-nm;\n                    if(!iT) {\n                        if(!found||g>bG) { found=true;bG=g;bM=m;bK=k;bTab=false; }\n                    } else if(nm<bestMs) {\n                        if(!found||!bTab||g>bG) { found=true;bG=g;bM=m;bK=k;bTab=true; }\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n            \n            if(!found) break;\n            \n            swap(cur[bM][bK],cur[bM][bK+1]);\n            curMs=eval(cur);\n            if(bK<(int)tab[bM].size()) tab[bM][bK]=iter+tenure;\n            iter++;\n            if(curMs>0&&curMs<bestMs) { bestMs=curMs; bestMO=cur; }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    // Output\n    auto bS=toStart(bestMO);\n    for(int j=0;j<J;j++) {\n        for(int p=0;p<(int)jM[j].size();p++) { if(p>0) cout<<\' \'; cout<<bS[j][p]<<\' \'<<jM[j][p]; }\n        cout<<\'\\n\';\n    }\n    return 0;\n}\n```\n\nHmm, let me review this one more time.\n\nOne issue: In the `eval` function, when processing node `u`:\n- I process jobSucc `v = jSucc[u]`\n- I process machSucc `w = wMS[u]`\n- I check `w != v` to avoid double-processing\n\nBut wait: if jobSucc and machSucc are the same node, I need to process it only once. Let me also think about edge cases:\n\n1. **Single job, single machine**: All ops of the single job on one machine. Should be straightforward.\n\n2. **Single op per job**: J jobs each with 1 op on some machine. Greedy assigns all to machines greedily.\n\n3. **All ops on same machine**: Serial execution. We can only change machine order. If op (j,p) and op (j,p+1) are on the same machine, they\'re in the machine order for that machine. But job order requires (j,p) before (j,p+1). If we swap them in machine order, (j,p+1) would come before (j,p) on the machine, but job order requires (j,p) first. This would create a cycle (machine constraint contradicts job constraint).\n\nSo swapping consecutive same-job ops on a machine → always creates a cycle → eval returns -1. We skip such swaps.\n\nOK that\'s handled correctly.\n\n5. **Empty job (T=0)**: A job with no ops. The greedy skips it (jobNext[j] >= size = 0). Let me write the final code.\n\nActually, I want to double-check one more thing. The `eval` function uses `wMS` (machine successor). Let me be clean and concise.\n\nOne optimization I want to add: for the eval function, the two loops `fill(wMP...)` and the machine order processing can be combined. Let me structure it clearly:\n\n```cpp\nint eval(const MO& mo, bool doL=false) {\n    // Step 1: Build machPred/machSucc from machine orders\n    fill(wMP.begin(),wMP.end(),-1);\n    fill(wMS.begin(),wMS.end(),-1);\n    for(int m=0;m<M;m++) {\n        const auto& v=mo[m];\n        for(size_t k=1;k<v.size();k++) {\n            int u=off[v[k].first]+v[k].second;\n            int w=off[v[k-1].first]+v[k-1].second;\n            wMP[u]=w; wMS[w]=u;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    // Step 2: Compute in-degrees (base + machine contribution)\n    copy(bDeg.begin(),bDeg.end(),wID.begin());\n    for(int i=0;i<nOps;i++) {\n        if(wMP[i]>=0) {\n            // Check if machine pred == job pred\n            int j=oJ[i],p=oP[i];\n            if(!(p>0 && wMP[i]==off[j]+p-1))\n                wID[i]++;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    // Step 3: BFS / Kahn\'s for forward pass\n    fill(wE.begin(),wE.end(),0);\n    int h=0,t=0,sz=0;\n    for(int i=0;i<nOps;i++) if(!wID[i]) wQ[t++]=i;\n    while(h<t) {\n        int u=wQ[h++]; sz++;\n        if(doL) wT[sz-1]=u;\n        int j=oJ[u],p=oP[u];\n        int et=wE[u]+jD[j][p];\n        int v=jSucc[u];\n        if(v>=0) { if(et>wE[v]) wE[v]=et; if(!--wID[v]) wQ[t++]=v; }\n        int w=wMS[u];\n        if(w>=0&&w!=v) { if(et>wE[w]) wE[w]=et; if(!--wID[w]) wQ[t++]=w; }\n    }\n    if(sz<nOps) return -1;\n    \n    // Step 4: Compute makespan\n    int ms=0;\n    for(int i=0;i<nOps;i++) { int e=wE[i]+jD[oJ[i]][oP[i]]; if(e>ms) ms=e; }\n    \n    // Step 5: (optional) Backward pass for LST\n    if(doL) {\n        fill(wL.begin(),wL.end(),ms);\n        for(int i=sz-1;i>=0;i--) {\n            int u=wT[i]; int j=oJ[u],p=oP[u];\n            int lu=wL[u]-jD[j][p];\n            if(p>0) { int v=off[j]+p-1; if(lu<wL[v]) wL[v]=lu; }\n            int w=wMP[u]; if(w>=0) { if(lu<wL[w]) wL[w]=lu; }\n        }\n        for(int i=0;i<nOps;i++) wL[i]-=jD[oJ[i]][oP[i]];\n    }\n    return ms;\n}\n```\n\nWait, there\'s a bug: `wT[sz-1]=u` should be `wT[sz-1]=u` but sz is already incremented before this. Here it is:\n\n```cpp\n#include <bits/stdc++.h>\nusing namespace std;\nusing namespace chrono;\n\nstatic int J, M, nOps;\nstatic vector<vector<int>> jM, jD;\nstatic vector<int> jW;\nstatic vector<int> off, oJ, oP, jSucc, bDeg;\n\nvoid init() {\n    off.resize(J+1,0);\n    for(int j=0;j<J;j++) off[j+1]=off[j]+(int)jM[j].size();\n    nOps=off[J];\n    oJ.resize(nOps); oP.resize(nOps); jSucc.assign(nOps,-1); bDeg.assign(nOps,0);\n    for(int j=0;j<J;j++)\n        for(int p=0;p<(int)jM[j].size();p++) {\n            int id=off[j]+p; oJ[id]=j; oP[id]=p;\n            if(p>0) bDeg[id]=1;\n            if(p+1<(int)jM[j].size()) jSucc[id]=id+1;\n        }\n}\n\nusing MO=vector<vector<pair<int,int>>>;\nstatic vector<int> wMP,wMS,wID,wE,wQ,wT,wL;\nvoid allocW() {\n    wMP.resize(nOps); wMS.resize(nOps); wID.resize(nOps);\n    wE.resize(nOps); wQ.resize(nOps); wT.resize(nOps); wL.resize(nOps);\n}\n\nint eval(const MO& mo, bool doL=false) {\n    fill(wMP.begin(),wMP.end(),-1); fill(wMS.begin(),wMS.end(),-1);\n    for(int m=0;m<M;m++) {\n        const auto& v=mo[m];\n        for(int k=1;k<(int)v.size();k++) {\n            int u=off[v[k].first]+v[k].second, w=off[v[k-1].first]+v[k-1].second;\n            wMP[u]=w; wMS[w]=u;\n        }\n    }\n    copy(bDeg.begin(),bDeg.end(),wID.begin());\n    for(int i=0;i<nOps;i++) if(wMP[i]>=0) {\n        int j=oJ[i],p=oP[i]; if(!(p>0&&wMP[i]==off[j]+p-1)) wID[i]++;\n    }\n    fill(wE.begin(),wE.end(),0);\n    int h=0,t=0,sz=0;\n    for(int i=0;i<nOps;i++) if(!wID[i]) wQ[t++]=i;\n    while(h<t) {\n        int u=wQ[h++]; if(doL) wT[sz]=u; sz++;\n        int j=oJ[u],p=oP[u],et=wE[u]+jD[j][p];\n        int v=jSucc[u];\n        if(v>=0) { if(et>wE[v]) wE[v]=et; if(!--wID[v]) wQ[t++]=v; }\n        int w=wMS[u];\n        if(w>=0&&w!=v) { if(et>wE[w]) wE[w]=et; if(!--wID[w]) wQ[t++]=w; }\n    }\n    if(sz<nOps) return -1;\n    int ms=0;\n    for(int i=0;i<nOps;i++) { int e=wE[i]+jD[oJ[i]][oP[i]]; if(e>ms) ms=e; }\n    if(doL) {\n        fill(wL.begin(),wL.end(),ms);\n        for(int i=sz-1;i>=0;i--) {\n            int u=wT[i]; int j=oJ[u],p=oP[u],lu=wL[u]-jD[j][p];\n            if(p>0) { int v=off[j]+p-1; if(lu<wL[v]) wL[v]=lu; }\n            if(wMP[u]>=0) { if(lu<wL[wMP[u]]) wL[wMP[u]]=lu; }\n        }\n        for(int i=0;i<nOps;i++) wL[i]-=jD[oJ[i]][oP[i]];\n    }\n    return ms;\n}\n\nMO toMO(const vector<vector<int>>& s) {\n    MO mo(M);\n    vector<vector<pair<int,pair<int,int>>>> tmp(M);\n    for(int j=0;j<J;j++)\n        for(int p=0;p<(int)jM[j].size();p++)\n            tmp[jM[j][p]].push_back({s[j][p],{j,p}});\n    for(int m=0;m<M;m++) {\n        sort(tmp[m].begin(),tmp[m].end());\n        for(auto& [t,jp]:tmp[m]) mo[m].push_back(jp);\n    }\n    return mo;\n}\n\nvector<vector<int>> toStart(const MO& mo) {\n    eval(mo);\n    vector<vector<int>> s(J);\n    for(int j=0;j<J;j++) {\n        s[j].resize(jM[j].size());\n        for(int p=0;p<(int)jM[j].size();p++) s[j][p]=wE[off[j]+p];\n    }\n    return s;\n}\n\nvector<vector<int>> greedy(int pri) {\n    vector<int> rW=jW;\n    vector<vector<int>> s(J); for(int j=0;j<J;j++) s[j].resize(jM[j].size());\n    vector<int> nx(J,0),rd(J,0),mf(M,0); vector<bool> um(M);\n    static vector<pair<int,int>> cands;\n    for(int sc=0;sc<nOps;) {\n        int t=INT_MAX;\n        for(int j=0;j<J;j++) { if(nx[j]>=(int)jM[j].size()) continue; int st=max(mf[jM[j][nx[j]]],rd[j]); if(st<t) t=st; }\n        cands.clear();\n        for(int j=0;j<J;j++) {\n            if(nx[j]>=(int)jM[j].size()) continue;\n            int m=jM[j][nx[j]];\n            if(max(mf[m],rd[j])!=t) continue;\n            int k=(pri==0)?-rW[j]:(pri==1)?jD[j][nx[j]]:-jD[j][nx[j]];\n            cands.push_back({k,j});\n        }\n        sort(cands.begin(),cands.end());\n        fill(um.begin(),um.end(),false);\n        for(auto [k,j]:cands) {\n            int p=nx[j],m=jM[j][p]; if(um[m]) continue; um[m]=true;\n            int d=jD[j][p]; s[j][p]=t; mf[m]=t+d; rd[j]=t+d; rW[j]-=d; nx[j]++; sc++;\n        }\n    }\n    return s;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    ios::sync_with_stdio(false); cin.tie(nullptr);\n    cin>>J>>M;\n    jM.resize(J); jD.resize(J); jW.resize(J,0);\n    for(int j=0;j<J;j++) {\n        int T; cin>>T; jM[j].resize(T); jD[j].resize(T);\n        for(int p=0;p<T;p++) { cin>>jM[j][p]>>jD[j][p]; jW[j]+=jD[j][p]; }\n    }\n    init(); allocW();\n    \n    // Greedy with multiple priority rules\n    MO bestMO; int bestMs=INT_MAX;\n    for(int pri=0;pri<3;pri++) {\n        auto s=greedy(pri);\n        auto mo=toMO(s);\n        int ms=eval(mo);\n        if(ms<bestMs) { bestMs=ms; bestMO=mo; }\n    }\n    \n    // Time-limited tabu search\n    auto t0=steady_clock::now();\n    auto elapsed=[&](){ return duration_cast<duration<double>>(steady_clock::now()-t0).count(); };\n    double tl=(nOps<=500)?8.0:(nOps<=5000)?5.0:(nOps<=20000)?2.0:0.5;\n    \n    if(nOps>0 && tl>0.05) {\n        int tenure=max(5,min(20,J/3+5));\n        MO cur=bestMO; int curMs=bestMs;\n        vector<vector<int>> tab(M);\n        for(int m=0;m<M;m++) tab[m].assign(max(1,(int)bestMO[m].size()),0);\n        int iter=0;\n        vector<int> cE(nOps),cL(nOps);\n        \n        while(elapsed()<tl) {\n            int ms=eval(cur,true); if(ms<0) break;\n            copy(wE.begin(),wE.end(),cE.begin());\n            copy(wL.begin(),wL.end(),cL.begin());\n            bool found=false; int bG=INT_MIN,bM=-1,bK=-1; bool bT=false;\n            \n            for(int m=0;m<M&&elapsed()<tl;m++) {\n                auto& v=cur[m]; int vsz=(int)v.size();\n                for(int k=0;k+1<vsz;k++) {\n                    int u=off[v[k].first]+v[k].second;\n                    int w=off[v[k+1].first]+v[k+1].second;\n                    if(nOps>300&&cE[u]!=cL[u]&&cE[w]!=cL[w]) continue;\n                    swap(v[k],v[k+1]);\n                    int nm=eval(cur);\n                    swap(v[k],v[k+1]);\n                    if(nm<0) continue;\n                    bool iT=(k<(int)tab[m].size()&&tab[m][k]>iter);\n                    int g=ms-nm;\n                    if(!iT) { if(!found||g>bG) {found=true;bG=g;bM=m;bK=k;bT=false;} }\n                    else if(nm<bestMs) { if(!found||!bT||g>bG) {found=true;bG=g;bM=m;bK=k;bT=true;} }\n                }\n            }\n            if(!found) break;\n            swap(cur[bM][bK],cur[bM][bK+1]);\n            curMs=eval(cur);\n            if(bK<(int)tab[bM].size()) tab[bM][bK]=iter+tenure;\n            iter++;\n            if(curMs>0&&curMs<bestMs) { bestMs=curMs; bestMO=cur; }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    auto bS=toStart(bestMO);\n    for(int j=0;j<J;j++) {\n        for(int p=0;p<(int)jM[j].size();p++) {\n            if(p>0) cout<<\' \';\n            cout<<bS[j][p]<<\' \'<<jM[j][p];\n        }\n        cout<<\'\\n\';\n    }\n    return 0;\n}\n```\n\nI think this is correct. That\'s not much, but better than nothing.\n\nFor nOps=5000: 5000² = 25M ops per iteration, at 10^9 ops/sec = 0.025s. With tl=5.0s: ~200 iterations. Excellent.\n\nActually, the number of evals per tabu iteration is not nOps² but rather #pairs * eval_cost = O(nOps) pairs * O(nOps) = O(nOps²). For nOps=500: O(250k) per iteration. Correct.\n\nBut with CP filter for nOps>300: only critical path pairs are evaluated. The critical path length is typically much shorter than nOps. Let\'s say it\'s O(sqrt(nOps)) or O(nOps/M). For nOps=5000, M=50: critical path length ≈ 100. So per iteration: 100 pairs * O(5000) = 500k ops ≈ 0.5ms. With tl=5.0s: ~10000 iterations. 👍\n\nFor nOps=20000, M=50: critical path ≈ 400 pairs * O(20000) = 8M ops ≈ 8ms. With tl=2.0s: ~250 iterations. OK.\n\nSo the CP filter significantly improves the number of iterations we can do.\n\nGreat, the design choices look sound.\n\nONE MORE THING: for the critical path filter, I use:\n```cpp\nif(nOps>300&&cE[u]!=cL[u]&&cE[w]!=cL[w]) continue;\n```\n\nThis says: skip if nOps>300 AND both u and w are NOT on the critical path.\n\nThe condition `cE[u]==cL[u]` means u is on the critical path.\n\nSo: `cE[u]!=cL[u]&&cE[w]!=cL[w]` means neither is on CP. We skip these.\n\nEquivalently: we include the pair if AT LEAST ONE of them is on the CP.\n\nThis is the "extended" critical path neighborhood, which is slightly larger than the "both on CP" neighborhood. It might include moves that don\'t reduce the makespan, but it also has better chance of finding improvements.\n\nFor strictness (both on CP), I\'d use:\n```cpp\nif(nOps>300&&!(cE[u]==cL[u]&&cE[w]==cL[w])) continue;\n```\n\nBut the extended version seems fine.\n\nOK I\'m truly done deliberating. Let me write and output the final code.\n\nLet me also double check: for large instances (nOps > 20000), `tl = 0.5`. With 3 greedy heuristics each taking O(J*nOps) time, and J*nOps can be up to 50M for the extreme case, the greedy takes ~0.05s × 3 = 0.15s. Plus some overhead for extractMO and eval. Total greedy time: ~0.5s (could be close to tl).\n\nHmm, for nOps=50k and J=1000: each greedy is O(J*nOps) = O(50M) ≈ 0.5s. Three greedy = 1.5s. Plus local search (tl=0.5s). Total ≈ 2s.\n\nThat should be fine for most time limits (usually 5-30 seconds in competitive programming).\n\nBut actually, let me reconsider the greedy time. For each of the nOps ops:\n- Scan J jobs: O(J)\n- Sort candidates: O(active_J * log(active_J)) where active_J ≤ J\n\nIn the worst case, all J jobs are active at every time step → O(J log J) per step → O(nOps * J log J) total.\n\nFor J=1000, nOps=50k: 50k * 1000 * 10 = 500M. At 10^9 simple ops/sec: 0.5s per greedy, 1.5s for 3. That\'s borderline.\n\nBut in practice, not all J jobs are active at the same time, so it\'s much faster.\n\nFor truly extreme cases, I should optimize the greedy. Options:\n1. Use a per-machine priority queue to avoid scanning all J jobs\n2. Use lazy evaluation\n\nBut for now, let me keep the simple approach and trust it\'s fast enough.\n\nAlright, here is the final code:\n\nActually, I want to add one more optimization to the greedy: instead of scanning all J jobs every iteration, maintain a per-machine priority queue of ready jobs.\n\nHere\'s the optimized greedy:\n\n```\nFor each machine m:\n    readyForM[m] = max-heap (by priority) of jobs whose next op is on m and whose rd[j] <= current_time\n\nFor each machine m:\n    schedule readyForM[m].top() if machine is free\n    advance time\n```\n\nBut coordinating across machines is complex. Let me use an event-driven approach:\n\n```\nevents = min-heap of (time, event_type, data)\nInitially:\n    For each job j: add event (0, JOB_READY, j)\n\nPer-machine ready queues: machReady[m] = priority_queue by -remWork (MWKR)\n\nProcess events:\n    (t, JOB_READY, j): // job j\'s next op is ready at time t\n        m = jM[j][nx[j]]\n        machReady[m].push((priority, j))\n        // If machine m is idle:\n        if(machFree[m] <= t):\n            // Schedule the best ready job\n            Schedule best from machReady[m] (those with rd[j] <= t)\n            // This is tricky because rd[j] might be > t for some jobs in machReady[m]\n```\n\nHmm, this is complex because the machine queue might have jobs that aren\'t actually ready yet. Let me simplify:\n\nFor each machine m:\n- When machine m becomes free at time t:\n  - Schedule the highest-priority job in machReady[m] that has rd[j] <= t\n  - If no such job, wait until the next job becomes ready\n\nThe "wait" part is handled by: when job j becomes ready (rd[j] updated), check if its next machine m is idle (machFree[m] <= rd[j]). If so, add a machine-free event at rd[j] for machine m.\n\nThis event-driven approach is O(nOps log nOps) total. Let me implement it:\n\nActually, you know what, for nOps=50k and J=1000, the simple O(J*nOps) = O(50M) approach is 0.5 seconds which is acceptable. Let me just use the simple approach and not over-engineer.\n\nFINAL FINAL CODE:\n\n```cpp\n#include <bits/stdc++.h>\nusing namespace std;\nusing namespace std::chrono;\n\nstatic int J, M, nOps;\nstatic vector<vector<int>> jMach, jDur;\nstatic vector<int> jTotWork;\nstatic vector<int> opOff; // opOff[j]: starting op id for job j\nstatic vector<int> opJob, opPos; // decode: opJob[id]=j, opPos[id]=p\nstatic vector<int> jobSucc; // jobSucc[id]: job successor op id, -1 if none\nstatic vector<int> baseDeg; // job-order contribution to in-degree\n\nvoid initProblem() {\n    opOff.resize(J+1, 0);\n    for(int j = 0; j < J; j++)\n        opOff[j+1] = opOff[j] + (int)jMach[j].size();\n    nOps = opOff[J];\n    \n    opJob.resize(nOps);\n    opPos.resize(nOps);\n    jobSucc.assign(nOps, -1);\n    baseDeg.assign(nOps, 0);\n    \n    for(int j = 0; j < J; j++) {\n        int sz = (int)jMach[j].size();\n        for(int p = 0; p < sz; p++) {\n            int id = opOff[j] + p;\n            opJob[id] = j;\n            opPos[id] = p;\n            if(p > 0) baseDeg[id] = 1; // has job predecessor\n            if(p + 1 < sz) jobSucc[id] = id + 1;\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nusing MO = vector<vector<pair<int,int>>>; // machine orders: mo[m] = list of (job, pos)\n\n// Reusable workspace for eval\nstatic vector<int> wMachPred, wMachSucc, wInDeg, wEst, wBfsQ, wTopoOrder, wLst;\n\nvoid allocWorkspace() {\n    wMachPred.resize(nOps);\n    wMachSucc.resize(nOps);\n    wInDeg.resize(nOps);\n    wEst.resize(nOps);\n    wBfsQ.resize(nOps);\n    wTopoOrder.resize(nOps);\n    wLst.resize(nOps);\n}\n\n// Evaluate schedule: compute EST (and optionally LST) from machine orders.\n// Returns makespan, or -1 if there\'s a cycle.\nint evalSchedule(const MO& mo, bool computeLST = false) {\n    // Build machine predecessor/successor arrays\n    fill(wMachPred.begin(), wMachPred.end(), -1);\n    fill(wMachSucc.begin(), wMachSucc.end(), -1);\n    for(int m = 0; m < M; m++) {\n        const auto& ord = mo[m];\n        for(int k = 1; k < (int)ord.size(); k++) {\n            int u = opOff[ord[k].first] + ord[k].second;\n            int v = opOff[ord[k-1].first] + ord[k-1].second;\n            wMachPred[u] = v;\n            wMachSucc[v] = u;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    // Compute in-degrees (job edges + machine edges, deduplicated)\n    copy(baseDeg.begin(), baseDeg.end(), wInDeg.begin());\n    for(int i = 0; i < nOps; i++) {\n        int mp = wMachPred[i];\n        if(mp >= 0) {\n            int j = opJob[i], p = opPos[i];\n            // Skip if machine pred == job pred\n            if(!(p > 0 && mp == opOff[j] + p - 1))\n                wInDeg[i]++;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    // BFS (Kahn\'s topological sort) to compute EST\n    fill(wEst.begin(), wEst.end(), 0);\n    int head = 0, tail = 0, topoSz = 0;\n    for(int i = 0; i < nOps; i++)\n        if(!wInDeg[i]) wBfsQ[tail++] = i;\n    \n    while(head < tail) {\n        int u = wBfsQ[head++];\n        if(computeLST) wTopoOrder[topoSz] = u;\n        topoSz++;\n        \n        int j = opJob[u], p = opPos[u];\n        int et = wEst[u] + jDur[j][p];\n        \n        int v = jobSucc[u];\n        if(v >= 0) {\n            if(et > wEst[v]) wEst[v] = et;\n            if(!--wInDeg[v]) wBfsQ[tail++] = v;\n        }\n        int w = wMachSucc[u];\n        if(w >= 0 && w != v) {\n            if(et > wEst[w]) wEst[w] = et;\n            if(!--wInDeg[w]) wBfsQ[tail++] = w;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    if(topoSz < nOps) return -1; // cycle detected\n    \n    // Compute makespan\n    int ms = 0;\n    for(int i = 0; i < nOps; i++) {\n        int e = wEst[i] + jDur[opJob[i]][opPos[i]];\n        if(e > ms) ms = e;\n    }\n    \n    // Backward pass to compute LST\n    if(computeLST) {\n        fill(wLst.begin(), wLst.end(), ms);\n        for(int i = topoSz - 1; i >= 0; i--) {\n            int u = wTopoOrder[i];\n            int j = opJob[u], p = opPos[u];\n            int lstU = wLst[u] - jDur[j][p]; // LFT[u] - dur[u] = LST[u]\n            if(p > 0) {\n                int v = opOff[j] + p - 1;\n                if(lstU < wLst[v]) wLst[v] = lstU;\n            }\n            int mp = wMachPred[u];\n            if(mp >= 0) {\n                if(lstU < wLst[mp]) wLst[mp] = lstU;\n            }\n        }\n        // Convert: wLst now stores LFT; convert to LST (= LFT - dur)\n        for(int i = 0; i < nOps; i++)\n            wLst[i] -= jDur[opJob[i]][opPos[i]];\n    }\n    \n    return ms;\n}\n\n// Extract machine orders from start-time schedule\nMO startToMO(const vector<vector<int>>& start) {\n    MO mo(M);\n    vector<vector<pair<int, pair<int,int>>>> tmp(M);\n    for(int j = 0; j < J; j++)\n        for(int p = 0; p < (int)jMach[j].size(); p++)\n            tmp[jMach[j][p]].push_back({start[j][p], {j, p}});\n    for(int m = 0; m < M; m++) {\n        sort(tmp[m].begin(), tmp[m].end());\n        for(auto& [t, jp] : tmp[m])\n            mo[m].push_back(jp);\n    }\n    return mo;\n}\n\n// Get start times from machine orders (via eval)\nvector<vector<int>> moToStart(const MO& mo) {\n    evalSchedule(mo); // fills wEst\n    vector<vector<int>> s(J);\n    for(int j = 0; j < J; j++) {\n        s[j].resize(jMach[j].size());\n        for(int p = 0; p < (int)jMach[j].size(); p++)\n            s[j][p] = wEst[opOff[j] + p];\n    }\n    return s;\n}\n\n// Greedy list scheduling\n// priority: 0=MWKR, 1=SPT, 2=LPT\nvector<vector<int>> greedySchedule(int priority) {\n    vector<int> remWork = jTotWork;\n    vector<vector<int>> s(J);\n    for(int j = 0; j < J; j++) s[j].resize(jMach[j].size());\n    \n    vector<int> nextOp(J, 0);     // next operation index for each job\n    vector<int> jobReady(J, 0);   // earliest start time for next op\n    vector<int> machFree(M, 0);   // earliest time machine is free\n    vector<bool> machUsed(M, false);\n    \n    static vector<pair<int,int>> cands; // (key, job)\n    \n    for(int scheduled = 0; scheduled < nOps; ) {\n        // Find minimum start time t\n        int t = INT_MAX;\n        for(int j = 0; j < J; j++) {\n            if(nextOp[j] >= (int)jMach[j].size()) continue;\n            int m = jMach[j][nextOp[j]];\n            int st = max(machFree[m], jobReady[j]);\n            if(st < t) t = st;\n        }\n        \n        // Collect ops that can start at time t\n        cands.clear();\n        for(int j = 0; j < J; j++) {\n            if(nextOp[j] >= (int)jMach[j].size()) continue;\n            int m = jMach[j][nextOp[j]];\n            if(max(machFree[m], jobReady[j]) != t) continue;\n            int key;\n            if(priority == 0) key = -remWork[j];       // MWKR (higher remWork = better)\n            else if(priority == 1) key = jDur[j][nextOp[j]]; // SPT\n            else key = -jDur[j][nextOp[j]];            // LPT\n            cands.push_back({key, j});\n        }\n        sort(cands.begin(), cands.end());\n        \n        // Schedule best op for each machine (no conflicts)\n        fill(machUsed.begin(), machUsed.end(), false);\n        for(auto [key, j] : cands) {\n            int p = nextOp[j];\n            int m = jMach[j][p];\n            if(machUsed[m]) continue;\n            machUsed[m] = true;\n            \n            int d = jDur[j][p];\n            s[j][p] = t;\n            machFree[m] = t + d;\n            jobReady[j] = t + d;\n            remWork[j] -= d;\n            nextOp[j]++;\n            scheduled++;\n        }\n    }\n    return s;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    ios::sync_with_stdio(false);\n    cin.tie(nullptr);\n    \n    // Read input\n    cin >> J >> M;\n    jMach.resize(J);\n    jDur.resize(J);\n    jTotWork.resize(J, 0);\n    \n    for(int j = 0; j < J; j++) {\n        int T;\n        cin >> T;\n        jMach[j].resize(T);\n        jDur[j].resize(T);\n        for(int p = 0; p < T; p++) {\n            cin >> jMach[j][p] >> jDur[j][p];\n            jTotWork[j] += jDur[j][p];\n        }\n    }\n    \n    initProblem();\n    allocWorkspace();\n    \n    // Run multiple greedy heuristics and pick best\n    MO bestMO;\n    int bestMs = INT_MAX;\n    \n    for(int pri = 0; pri < 3; pri++) {\n        auto s = greedySchedule(pri);\n        auto mo = startToMO(s);\n        int ms = evalSchedule(mo);\n        if(ms < bestMs) {\n            bestMs = ms;\n            bestMO = mo;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    // Tabu search improvement (time-limited)\n    auto t0 = steady_clock::now();\n    auto elapsed = [&]() -> double {\n        return duration_cast<duration<double>>(steady_clock::now() - t0).count();\n    };\n    \n    double timeLimit;\n    if(nOps <= 500)       timeLimit = 8.0;\n    else if(nOps <= 5000) timeLimit = 5.0;\n    else if(nOps <= 20000) timeLimit = 2.0;\n    else                  timeLimit = 0.5;\n    \n    if(nOps > 0) {\n        int tenure = max(5, min(20, J/3 + 5));\n        MO curMO = bestMO;\n        int curMs = bestMs;\n        \n        // Tabu list: tab[m][k] = iteration when swap(m, k, k+1) is allowed again\n        vector<vector<int>> tab(M);\n        for(int m = 0; m < M; m++)\n            tab[m].assign(max(1, (int)bestMO[m].size()), 0);\n        \n        int iter = 0;\n        vector<int> curEst(nOps), curLst(nOps);\n        \n        while(elapsed() < timeLimit) {\n            int ms = evalSchedule(curMO, true);\n            if(ms < 0) break;\n            \n            copy(wEst.begin(), wEst.end(), curEst.begin());\n            copy(wLst.begin(), wLst.end(), curLst.begin());\n            \n            bool found = false;\n            int bestGain = INT_MIN, bestM = -1, bestK = -1;\n            bool bestIsTabu = false;\n            \n            for(int m = 0; m < M && elapsed() < timeLimit; m++) {\n                auto& ord = curMO[m];\n                int vsz = (int)ord.size();\n                for(int k = 0; k + 1 < vsz; k++) {\n                    int u = opOff[ord[k].first] + ord[k].second;\n                    int w = opOff[ord[k+1].first] + ord[k+1].second;\n                    \n                    // Critical path filter for larger instances\n                    if(nOps > 300) {\n                        bool uOnCP = (curEst[u] == curLst[u]);\n                        bool wOnCP = (curEst[w] == curLst[w]);\n                        if(!uOnCP && !wOnCP) continue;\n                    }\n                    \n                    // Try swap\n                    swap(ord[k], ord[k+1]);\n                    int newMs = evalSchedule(curMO);\n                    swap(ord[k], ord[k+1]); // revert\n                    \n                    if(newMs < 0) continue; // skip if creates cycle\n                    \n                    bool isTabu = (k < (int)tab[m].size() && tab[m][k] > iter);\n                    int gain = ms - newMs;\n                    \n                    if(!isTabu) {\n                        if(!found || gain > bestGain) {\n                            found = true;\n                            bestGain = gain;\n                            bestM = m; bestK = k;\n                            bestIsTabu = false;\n                        }\n                    } else if(newMs < bestMs) { // aspiration criterion\n                        if(!found || !bestIsTabu || gain > bestGain) {\n                            found = true;\n                            bestGain = gain;\n                            bestM = m; bestK = k;\n                            bestIsTabu = true;\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n            \n            if(!found) break; // no improving move found (stuck)\n            \n            // Apply best move\n            swap(curMO[bestM][bestK], curMO[bestM][bestK+1]);\n            curMs = evalSchedule(curMO);\n            if(bestK < (int)tab[bestM].size())\n                tab[bestM][bestK] = iter + tenure;\n            iter++;\n            \n            if(curMs > 0 && curMs < bestMs) {\n                bestMs = curMs;\n                bestMO = curMO;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    // Get start times from best solution\n    auto bestStart = moToStart(bestMO);\n    \n    // Output\n    for(int j = 0; j < J; j++) {\n        for(int p = 0; p < (int)jMach[j].size(); p++) {\n            if(p > 0) cout << \' \';\n            cout << bestStart[j][p] << \' \' << jMach[j][p];\n        }\n        cout << \'\\n\';\n    }\n    \n    return 0;\n}\n```\n\nWait, there\'s a potential issue: when `bestMs = INT_MAX` and no greedy solution was found (nOps=0). Let me handle:\n\nIf J=0 or all T=0: nOps=0, greedy returns empty start arrays, toMO returns empty MO, evalSchedule returns 0 (no ops), bestMs=0, bestMO is valid empty MO. Output: nothing (loops don\'t run). ✓\n\nIf J>0 and some T=0: those jobs produce no ops. Output for those jobs: empty line (p loop doesn\'t run). ✓\n\nOK I think this is solid. Let me also reconsider if the code compiles under MSVC with C++20. Let me double-check the structured bindings:\n\n```cpp\nfor(auto& [t, jp] : tmp[m])\n    mo[m].push_back(jp);\n```\n\nHere `tmp[m]` is `vector<pair<int, pair<int,int>>>`. Each element is `pair<int, pair<int,int>>`. Binding: `t` = first (int), `jp` = second (pair<int,int>). ✓\n\n```cpp\nfor(auto [key, j] : cands) {\n```\n\n`cands` is `vector<pair<int,int>>`. Binding: `key` = first, `j` = second. ✓\n\nI think the code is correct and compiles. Let me finalize.\n\nActually, I just realized there might be a performance issue with the inner loop time check. The `elapsed()` function calls `steady_clock::now()` which involves a system call. For the inner k-loop, calling this every time might be slow. Let me check only in the outer machine loop:\n\n```cpp\nfor(int m = 0; m < M && elapsed() < timeLimit; m++) {\n    ...\n    for(int k = 0; k + 1 < vsz; k++) {\n        // no time check here\n        ...\n    }\n}\n```\n\nI already have `&& elapsed() < timeLimit` in the machine loop. This checks at most M times per tabu iteration. For M=50: 50 calls to `elapsed()` per iteration. That\'s fine.\n\nThe issue: what if `vsz` (size of machine order) is very large and the k-loop takes a long time? For example, machine 0 has 1000 ops and each eval takes 1ms. The k-loop takes 1000ms = 1s without a time check. This could overshoot significantly.\n\nFor large instances (nOps > 5000), the time limit is small (2s or 0.5s). If one machine order has 1000 ops and each eval takes 5ms (for nOps=5000), the k-loop for that machine takes 5000ms = 5s, way over the time limit.\n\nFix: add a time check inside the k-loop, but only every N iterations:\n\n```cpp\nfor(int k = 0; k + 1 < vsz; k++) {\n    if(k % 20 == 0 && elapsed() >= timeLimit) goto doneSearch;\n    ...\n}\n```\n\nThis checks every 20 k-iterations. For each check: one chrono call. For 1000 k-iterations: 50 checks, ~50 chrono calls. Overhead is minimal.\n\nAlternatively, pass a reference to an "interrupt" flag:\n\n```cpp\nfor(int m = 0; m < M; m++) {\n    auto& ord = curMO[m];\n    int vsz = (int)ord.size();\n    for(int k = 0; k + 1 < vsz; k++) {\n        if((k & 31) == 0 && elapsed() >= timeLimit) goto doneSearch;\n        ...\n    }\n}\ndoneSearch:;\n```\n\nUsing `(k & 31) == 0` is equivalent to `k % 32 == 0` but faster.\n\nLet me add this.\n\nAlso, I need to declare `doneSearch` correctly in C++. Using `goto` and labels is fine:\n\n```cpp\nbool timeUp = false;\nfor(int m = 0; m < M && !timeUp; m++) {\n    auto& ord = curMO[m];\n    int vsz = (int)ord.size();\n    for(int k = 0; k + 1 < vsz; k++) {\n        if((k & 15) == 0 && elapsed() >= timeLimit) { timeUp = true; break; }\n        ...\n    }\n}\nif(timeUp) break; // break out of tabu search while loop\n```\n\nThis is cleaner than goto.\n\nLet me add this to the final code.\n\nOK I\'ll finalize now. Here\'s the complete code:\n\n[Code as above with the `timeUp` check]\n\nActually, let me restructure the tabu search loop to handle the timing properly:\n\n```cpp\nouter:\nwhile(elapsed() < timeLimit) {\n    int ms = evalSchedule(curMO, true);\n    if(ms < 0) break;\n    copy(wEst.begin(), wEst.end(), curEst.begin());\n    copy(wLst.begin(), wLst.end(), curLst.begin());\n    \n    bool found = false;\n    int bestGain = INT_MIN, bestM = -1, bestK = -1;\n    bool bestIsTabu = false;\n    \n    for(int m = 0; m < M && !done; m++) {\n        for(int k = 0; k + 1 < vsz && !done; k++) {\n            if((k & 15) == 0 && elapsed() >= timeLimit) { done = true; break; }\n            // ...\n        }\n    }\n    if(done) break;\n    // apply best move\n}\n```\n\nLet me use the `goto` approach for simplicity:\n\n```cpp\nwhile(elapsed() < timeLimit) {\n    // ...\n    for(int m = 0; m < M; m++) {\n        for(int k = 0; ...; k++) {\n            if((k & 15) == 0 && elapsed() >= timeLimit) goto doneSearch;\n            // ...\n        }\n    }\n    // ...\n}\ndoneSearch:;\n```\n\nAlright let me put together the TRULY final code:\n\n```cpp\n#include <bits/stdc++.h>\nusing namespace std;\nusing namespace std::chrono;\n\nstatic int J, M, nOps;\nstatic vector<vector<int>> jMach, jDur;\nstatic vector<int> jTotWork;\nstatic vector<int> opOff, opJob, opPos, jobSuccArr, baseDeg;\n\nvoid initProblem() {\n    opOff.resize(J+1, 0);\n    for(int j = 0; j < J; j++)\n        opOff[j+1] = opOff[j] + (int)jMach[j].size();\n    nOps = opOff[J];\n    opJob.resize(nOps); opPos.resize(nOps);\n    jobSuccArr.assign(nOps, -1); baseDeg.assign(nOps, 0);\n    for(int j = 0; In C++, jumping over variable declarations with goto can be an error if the variable has a non-trivial constructor. In my case, the variables in the while loop body (like `ms`, `found`, etc.) are all simple types or declared before the goto. Let me use slightly longer names for readability.\n\nAlso, I realize there\'s another issue: the greedy scheduler might not be correct for the case where no ops are ready at all (which shouldn\'t happen, but let me double-check).\n\nIn the greedy:\n```cpp\nint t=INT_MAX;\nfor(int j=0;j<J;j++) {\n    if(nx[j]>=(int)jMach[j].size()) continue;\n    int st=max(mf[jMach[j][nx[j]]],rd[j]);\n    if(st<t) t=st;\n}\n```\n\nAfter the loop, if `t == INT_MAX`, it means all jobs are completed (no remaining ops). But we\'re in the `for(int sc=0;sc<nOps;)` loop, so `sc < nOps` implies there ARE remaining ops. If `t == INT_MAX` despite `sc < nOps`, it means something went wrong.\n\nThis can\'t happen if the problem is well-formed: each job has `T ≥ 1` ops, and we process them in order. When `sc < nOps`, there exists at least one job with `nx[j] < |ops|`. For that job, the ready time is `max(mf[m], rd[j])` which is finite. So `t < INT_MAX`. ✓\n\nOK I\'m done. Let me write the final code with clear but concise names.\n\nLet me also double-check one edge case in `ev`: what if M=0? Then the machPred/machSucc loops don\'t execute, and we have only job order constraints. For each op, inDeg = baseDeg (from job constraints). The BFS processes ops in job order. No machine conflicts. This should work correctly.\n\nBut if M=0 and J>0 with some T>0: the problem says tasks must run on a machine. If M=0, there are no machines, so no tasks can run. This would be an invalid input. We\'ll ignore this edge case.\n\nAnd if M>0 but some jobs have tasks on non-existent machines (machine id >= M): undefined behavior. We trust the input is valid per the problem statement.\n\nAlright, FINAL code:\n\nI\'ll write it once more, cleanly. Here are the key decisions:\n\n1. Let me just commit to the code I have (with the `stop` flag) and finalize it. It\'s correct and handles all the cases.\n\nActually, there\'s one more potential issue: the `wMS[v[k-1].first]+v[k-1].second` in the `ev` function. If `v[k-1]` is a `pair<int,int>` with `.first = job` and `.second = position`, then `opOff[v[k-1].first] + v[k-1].second` gives the op id. This is correct.\n\nBut `opOff` is indexed by job id. For job id 0 to J-1. If `v[k-1].first` is out of range, undefined behavior. But machine orders only contain valid (job, position) pairs. ✓\n\nOK let me finalize the code. The version I have above looks correct. Let me clean it up one more time with proper formatting, and that\'s the final answer.\n\nOh wait, I just noticed: in the backward pass, I initialize `wL` with `ms` (the makespan). Then for each node in reverse topological order, I compute `lu = wL[u] - jDur[j][p]` which is the "latest start time" of `u`. I then update predecessors:\n- Job predecessor: `wL[opOff[j]+p-1] = min(wL[opOff[j]+p-1], lu)`\n- Machine predecessor: `wL[wMP[u]] = min(wL[wMP[u]], lu)`\n\nBut wait: `wL` was initialized as the "latest finish time" (LFT = ms for all ops initially). The update `lu = wL[u] - dur[u]` computes LST from LFT. Then we update `wL[pred] = min(wL[pred], lu)`. This is saying LFT[pred] ≤ LST[u], which is correct (predecessor must finish before u starts at LST[u]).\n\nAt the end, I convert LFT to LST: `wL[i] -= jDur[...]`. But at this point, `wL[i]` is LFT (updated from initial ms by the backward pass). Subtracting duration gives LST. ✓\n\nBut hold on: during the backward pass, some `wL[i]` values were already updated to be LST rather than LFT (if they were updated multiple times). Wait no: the update sets `wL[pred] = min(wL[pred], lu)` where `lu = LST[u]`. We\'re saying `LFT[pred] ≤ LST[u]`. So `wL[pred]` represents `LFT[pred]` throughout the backward pass. The final conversion `wL[i] -= dur[i]` gives `LST[i] = LFT[i] - dur[i]`. ✓\n\nYes, this is correct! The wL array stores LFT during the backward pass, and we convert to LST at the end.\n\nAlright, everything checks out. Let me write the final code now:\n\n```cpp\n#include <bits/stdc++.h>\nusing namespace std;\nusing namespace std::chrono;\n\nstatic int J, M, nOps;\nstatic vector<vector<int>> jMach, jDur;\nstatic vector<int> jTotWork;\nstatic vector<int> opOff, opJob, opPos;\nstatic vector<int> jobSucc; // job successor op id\nstatic vector<int> baseDeg; // in-degree from job edges\n\nvoid setup() {\n    opOff.assign(J+1, 0);\n    for(int j = 0; j < J; j++)\n        opOff[j+1] = opOff[j] + (int)jMach[j].size();\n    nOps = opOff[J];\n    opJob.resize(nOps);\n    opPos.resize(nOps);\n    jobSucc.assign(nOps, -1);\n    baseDeg.assign(nOps, 0);\n    for(int j = 0; j < J; j++) {\n        int sz = (int)jMach[j].size();\n        for(int p = 0; p < sz; p++) {\n            int id = opOff[j] + p;\n            opJob[id] = j;\n            opPos[id] = p;\n            if(p > 0) baseDeg[id] = 1;\n            if(p + 1 < sz) jobSucc[id] = id + 1;\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nusing MO = vector<vector<pair<int,int>>>; // mo[m] = list of (job, pos)\n\n// Working arrays for eval\nstatic vector<int> wMachPred, wMachSucc, wInDeg, wEST, wBfsQ, wTopo, wLST;\n\nvoid allocWorkspace() {\n    wMachPred.resize(nOps); wMachSucc.resize(nOps);\n    wInDeg.resize(nOps); wEST.resize(nOps);\n    wBfsQ.resize(nOps); wTopo.resize(nOps); wLST.resize(nOps);\n}\n\n// Evaluate schedule from machine orders.\n// Returns makespan, or -1 if cycle.\n// If doLST=true, also computes LST in wLST.\nint evalSched(const MO& mo, bool doLST = false) {\n    // Build machine predecessor/successor\n    fill(wMachPred.begin(), wMachPred.end(), -1);\n    fill(wMachSucc.begin(), wMachSucc.end(), -1);\n    for(int m = 0; m < M; m++) {\n        const auto& ord = mo[m];\n        for(int k = 1; k < (int)ord.size(); k++) {\n            int u = opOff[ord[k].first] + ord[k].second;\n            int v = opOff[ord[k-1].first] + ord[k-1].second;\n            wMachPred[u] = v;\n            wMachSucc[v] = u;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    // Compute in-degrees\n    copy(baseDeg.begin(), baseDeg.end(), wInDeg.begin());\n    for(int i = 0; i < nOps; i++) {\n        int mp = wMachPred[i];\n        if(mp >= 0) {\n            int j = opJob[i], p = opPos[i];\n            // Skip if same as job predecessor (deduplicate)\n            if(!(p > 0 && mp == opOff[j] + p - 1))\n                wInDeg[i]++;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    // Forward BFS (Kahn\'s)\n    fill(wEST.begin(), wEST.end(), 0);\n    int head = 0, tail = 0, processed = 0;\n    for(int i = 0; i < nOps; i++)\n        if(!wInDeg[i]) wBfsQ[tail++] = i;\n    \n    while(head < tail) {\n        int u = wBfsQ[head++];\n        if(doLST) wTopo[processed] = u;\n        processed++;\n        \n        int j = opJob[u], p = opPos[u];\n        int et = wEST[u] + jDur[j][p];\n        \n        // Job successor\n        int v = jobSucc[u];\n        if(v >= 0) {\n            if(et > wEST[v]) wEST[v] = et;\n            if(!--wInDeg[v]) wBfsQ[tail++] = v;\n        }\n        // Machine successor (if different from job successor)\n        int w = wMachSucc[u];\n        if(w >= 0 && w != v) {\n            if(et > wEST[w]) wEST[w] = et;\n            if(!--wInDeg[w]) wBfsQ[tail++] = w;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    if(processed < nOps) return -1; // cycle\n    \n    int ms = 0;\n    for(int i = 0; i < nOps; i++) {\n        int e = wEST[i] + jDur[opJob[i]][opPos[i]];\n        if(e > ms) ms = e;\n    }\n    \n    // Backward pass for LST\n    if(doLST) {\n        fill(wLST.begin(), wLST.end(), ms); // initialize LFT to ms\n        for(int i = processed - 1; i >= 0; i--) {\n            int u = wTopo[i];\n            int j = opJob[u], p = opPos[u];\n            int lstU = wLST[u] - jDur[j][p]; // LFT - dur = LST\n            // Update job predecessor\'s LFT\n            if(p > 0) {\n                int v = opOff[j] + p - 1;\n                if(lstU < wLST[v]) wLST[v] = lstU;\n            }\n            // Update machine predecessor\'s LFT\n            int mp = wMachPred[u];\n            if(mp >= 0 && lstU < wLST[mp]) wLST[mp] = lstU;\n        }\n        // Convert LFT to LST\n        for(int i = 0; i < nOps; i++)\n            wLST[i] -= jDur[opJob[i]][opPos[i]];\n    }\n    \n    return ms;\n}\n\n// Convert start-time schedule to machine orders\nMO startToMO(const vector<vector<int>>& s) {\n    MO mo(M);\n    vector<vector<pair<int, pair<int,int>>>> tmp(M);\n    for(int j = 0; j < J; j++)\n        for(int p = 0; p < (int)jMach[j].size(); p++)\n            tmp[jMach[j][p]].push_back({s[j][p], {j, p}});\n    for(int m = 0; m < M; m++) {\n        sort(tmp[m].begin(), tmp[m].end());\n        for(auto& [t, jp] : tmp[m])\n            mo[m].push_back(jp);\n    }\n    return mo;\n}\n\n// Get start times from machine orders\nvector<vector<int>> moToStart(const MO& mo) {\n    evalSched(mo);\n    vector<vector<int>> s(J);\n    for(int j = 0; j < J; j++) {\n        s[j].resize(jMach[j].size());\n        for(int p = 0; p < (int)jMach[j].size(); p++)\n            s[j][p] = wEST[opOff[j] + p];\n    }\n    return s;\n}\n\n// Greedy list scheduling\n// priority: 0=MWKR, 1=SPT, 2=LPT\nvector<vector<int>> greedy(int priority) {\n    vector<int> remWork = jTotWork;\n    vector<vector<int>> s(J);\n    for(int j = 0; j < J; j++) s[j].resize(jMach[j].size());\n    \n    vector<int> nextOp(J, 0);\n    vector<int> jobReady(J, 0);\n    vector<int> machFree(M, 0);\n    vector<bool> machUsed(M, false);\n    \n    static vector<pair<int,int>> cands;\n    \n    for(int scheduled = 0; scheduled < nOps; ) {\n        // Find earliest possible start time\n        int t = INT_MAX;\n        for(int j = 0; j < J; j++) {\n            if(nextOp[j] >= (int)jMach[j].size()) continue;\n            int m = jMach[j][nextOp[j]];\n            int st = max(machFree[m], jobReady[j]);\n            if(st < t) t = st;\n        }\n        \n        // Collect operations ready at time t\n        cands.clear();\n        for(int j = 0; j < J; j++) {\n            if(nextOp[j] >= (int)jMach[j].size()) continue;\n            int m = jMach[j][nextOp[j]];\n            if(max(machFree[m], jobReady[j]) != t) continue;\n            int key;\n            if(priority == 0)      key = -remWork[j];      // MWKR\n            else if(priority == 1) key = jDur[j][nextOp[j]]; // SPT\n            else                   key = -jDur[j][nextOp[j]]; // LPT\n            cands.push_back({key, j});\n        }\n        sort(cands.begin(), cands.end());\n        \n        fill(machUsed.begin(), machUsed.end(), false);\n        for(auto [key, j] : cands) {\n            int p = nextOp[j], m = jMach[j][p];\n            if(machUsed[m]) continue;\n            machUsed[m] = true;\n            int d = jDur[j][p];\n            s[j][p] = t;\n            machFree[m] = t + d;\n            jobReady[j] = t + d;\n            remWork[j] -= d;\n            nextOp[j]++;\n            scheduled++;\n        }\n    }\n    return s;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    ios::sync_with_stdio(false);\n    cin.tie(nullptr);\n    \n    cin >> J >> M;\n    jMach.resize(J); jDur.resize(J); jTotWork.resize(J, 0);\n    for(int j = 0; j < J; j++) {\n        int T; cin >> T;\n        jMach[j].resize(T); jDur[j].resize(T);\n        for(int p = 0; p < T; p++) {\n            cin >> jMach[j][p] >> jDur[j][p];\n            jTotWork[j] += jDur[j][p];\n        }\n    }\n    \n    setup();\n    allocWorkspace();\n    \n    // Find best greedy solution among multiple priority rules\n    MO bestMO;\n    int bestMs = INT_MAX;\n    \n    if(nOps == 0) {\n        bestMs = 0;\n        bestMO = MO(M);\n    } else {\n        for(int pri = 0; pri < 3; pri++) {\n            auto s = greedy(pri);\n            auto mo = startToMO(s);\n            int ms = evalSched(mo);\n            if(ms < bestMs) {\n                bestMs = ms;\n                bestMO = mo;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    // Time-limited tabu search\n    auto t0 = steady_clock::now();\n    auto elapsed = [&]() -> double {\n        return duration_cast<duration<double>>(steady_clock::now() - t0).count();\n    };\n    \n    // Adaptive time limit based on problem size\n    double timeLimit;\n    if(nOps <= 500)        timeLimit = 8.0;\n    else if(nOps <= 5000)  timeLimit = 5.0;\n    else if(nOps <= 20000) timeLimit = 2.0;\n    else                   timeLimit = 0.5;\n    \n    if(nOps > 0 && timeLimit > 0.05) {\n        int tenure = max(5, min(20, J / 3 + 5));\n        MO curMO = bestMO;\n        int curMs = bestMs;\n        \n        // Tabu list: tab[m][k] = iteration number when move (m, k) becomes allowed\n        vector<vector<int>> tab(M);\n        for(int m = 0; m < M; m++)\n            tab[m].assign(max(1, (int)bestMO[m].size()), 0);\n        \n        int iteration = 0;\n        vector<int> curEST(nOps), curLST(nOps);\n        bool stop = false;\n        \n        while(!stop && elapsed() < timeLimit) {\n            int ms = evalSched(curMO, true);\n            if(ms < 0) break;\n            \n            // Save current solution\'s EST and LST\n            copy(wEST.begin(), wEST.end(), curEST.begin());\n            copy(wLST.begin(), wLST.end(), curLST.begin());\n            \n            bool found = false;\n            int bestGain = INT_MIN, bestM = -1, bestK = -1;\n            bool bestIsTabu = false;\n            \n            for(int m = 0; m < M && !stop; m++) {\n                auto& ord = curMO[m];\n                int vsz = (int)ord.size();\n                for(int k = 0; k + 1 < vsz; k++) {\n                    // Periodic time check\n                    if((k & 15) == 0 && elapsed() >= timeLimit) {\n                        stop = true; break;\n                    }\n                    \n                    int u = opOff[ord[k].first] + ord[k].second;\n                    int w = opOff[ord[k+1].first] + ord[k+1].second;\n                    \n                    // Critical path filter for larger instances\n                    if(nOps > 300) {\n                        bool uOnCP = (curEST[u] == curLST[u]);\n                        bool wOnCP = (curEST[w] == curLST[w]);\n                        if(!uOnCP && !wOnCP) continue;\n                    }\n                    \n                    // Try this swap\n                    swap(ord[k], ord[k+1]);\n                    int newMs = evalSched(curMO);\n                    swap(ord[k], ord[k+1]); // revert\n                    \n                    if(newMs < 0) continue; // creates cycle, skip\n                    \n                    bool isTabu = (k < (int)tab[m].size() && tab[m][k] > iteration);\n                    int gain = ms - newMs;\n                    \n                    if(!isTabu) {\n                        if(!found || gain > bestGain) {\n                            found = true;\n                            bestGain = gain;\n                            bestM = m; bestK = k;\n                            bestIsTabu = false;\n                        }\n                    } else if(newMs < bestMs) { // aspiration\n                        if(!found || !bestIsTabu || gain > bestGain) {\n                            found = true;\n                            bestGain = gain;\n                            bestM = m; bestK = k;\n                            bestIsTabu = true;\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n            \n            if(stop || !found) break;\n            \n            // Apply the best move\n            swap(curMO[bestM][bestK], curMO[bestM][bestK+1]);\n            curMs = evalSched(curMO);\n            if(bestK < (int)tab[bestM].size())\n                tab[bestM][bestK] = iteration + tenure;\n            iteration++;\n            \n            if(curMs > 0 && curMs < bestMs) {\n                bestMs = curMs;\n                bestMO = curMO;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    // Output start times\n    auto bestStart = moToStart(bestMO);\n    for(int j = 0; j < J; j++) {\n        for(int p = 0; p < (int)jMach[j].size(); p++) {\n            if(p > 0) cout << \' \';\n            cout << bestStart[j][p] << \' \' << jMach[j][p];\n        }\n        cout << \'\\n\';\n    }\n    \n    return 0;\n}\n```\n\nI think this is my final version. In machine order, (j1,p1) comes before (j2,p2). Machine constraint: (j1,p1) must finish before (j2,p2) starts. Finish time of (j1,p1) = t1 + dur(j1,p1). Since t2 ≥ t1 + dur(j1,p1) (the machine was free at t2 because the greedy ensures no overlap), the constraint is satisfied. ✓\n\nSo the greedy never produces a cycle. `evalSched(mo) >= 0` always. ✓\n\nFor the tabu search, we check `if(newMs < 0) continue` to skip cycle-creating swaps. ✓\n\nOK great. The code is correct and handles all edge cases. Final answer!\n\nWait wait wait. I just realized: in the `evalSched` function, the backward pass might have an issue. After the backward pass, `wLST[i]` should be the LATEST START TIME for op i. An op is on the critical path if `wEST[i] == wLST[i]`.\n\nBut let me re-examine the backward pass:\n- Initialize: `wLST[i] = ms` (this is LFT initially, we\'ll convert at the end)\n- Process in reverse topo order:\n  - For op u with LFT = wLST[u]: LST[u] = LFT[u] - dur[u] = wLST[u] - dur\n  - Update pred\'s LFT: LFT[pred] ≤ LST[u]\n  - So: wLST[pred] = min(wLST[pred], LST[u]) = min(wLST[pred], wLST[u] - dur[u])\n- Convert: wLST[i] -= dur[i] (converts from LFT to LST)\n\nBut there\'s a subtlety: when we update `wLST[pred] = min(wLST[pred], wLST[u] - dur[u])`, the `wLST[u]` at this point is the LFT of u (already updated by its successors). And `wLST[u] - dur[u]` is the LST of u. So we\'re saying: LFT[pred] ≤ LST[u]. This is correct: pred must finish before u starts at its latest.\n\nLet me trace through the example again:\n\nAfter forward pass:\n- wEST = [0, 3, 0, 3]\n- makespan = 7\n\nInitialize wLST = [7, 7, 7, 7]\n\nReverse topo order: for the example, topo order was [0, 2, 3, 1] (based on BFS). Reverse: [1, 3, 2, 0].\n\nProcess op 1 (j=0, p=1, dur=2):\n- LST[1] = wLST[1] - 2 = 7 - 2 = 5\n- Job pred: j=0, p=0 → id=0. wLST[0] = min(7, 5) = 5.\n- Machine pred: wMP[1] = 2 (op (1,0)=2). wLST[2] = min(7, 5) = 5.\n\nProcess op 3 (j=1, p=1, dur=4):\n- LST[3] = wLST[3] - 4 = 7 - 4 = 3\n- Job pred: j=1, p=0 → id=2. wLST[2] = min(5, 3) = 3.\n- Machine pred: wMP[3] = 0 (op (0,0)=0). wLST[0] = min(5, 3) = 3.\n\nProcess op 2 (j=1, p=0, dur=2):\n- LST[2] = wLST[2] - 2 = 3 - 2 = 1\n- No job pred (p=0).\n- No machine pred (wMP[2]=-1).\n\nProcess op 0 (j=0, p=0, dur=3):\n- LST[0] = wLST[0] - 3 = 3 - 3 = 0\n- No job pred (p=0).\n- No machine pred (wMP[0]=-1).\n\nConvert LFT to LST:\n- wLST[0] -= 3: 3 - 3 = 0\n- wLST[1] -= 2: 7 - 2 = 5\n- wLST[2] -= 2: 3 - 2 = 1\n- wLST[3] -= 4: 7 - 4 = 3\n\nSo wLST = [0, 5, 1, 3]\n\nCritical path (wEST[i] == wLST[i]):\n- Op 0: 0 == 0 ✓\n- Op 1: 3 == 5? ✗\n- Op 2: 0 == 1? ✗\n- Op 3: 3 == 3 ✓\n\nThis matches my earlier analysis. ✓\n\nThe code is correct.\n\nAlright, I\'m truly done. The final code is what I wrote above. Let me format it properly and submit.\n\nOne potential issue: MSVC might complain about `auto [j, p]` structured bindings in some contexts. The code above (the complete, clean version) is my final answer.', 'cpp_code': "#include <bits/stdc++.h>\nusing namespace std;\nusing namespace std::chrono;\n\nstatic int J, M, nOps;\nstatic vector<vector<int>> jMach, jDur;\nstatic vector<int> jTotWork;\nstatic vector<int> opOff, opJob, opPos;\nstatic vector<int> jobSucc;\nstatic vector<int> baseDeg;\n\nvoid setup() {\n    opOff.assign(J+1, 0);\n    for(int j = 0;
